small	Though not entirely satisfied, the explorers\x0d\nmanage to secure a modest supply of\x0d\nedible matter for their home planet.\x0d\n\x0d\nYet, still they wonder: Can this handful of\x0d\nseeds really bring salvation to the people\x0d\nof Koppai?\x0d\n\x0d\nEven if they carefully cultivate the seeds\x0d\nthey've harvested, it may not be enough to\x0d\nsupport the entire population.\x0d\n\x0d\nThis thought hovers over the explorers as\x0d\nthey embark on their journey home. middle	And so the intrepid explorers succeed in\x0d\nsecuring a reasonable supply of edible\x0d\nmatter for their home planet.\x0d\n\x0d\nIf they carefully cultivate the seeds they've\x0d\nharvested, it just may bring salvation to\x0d\nthe people of Koppai.\x0d\n\x0d\nHowever, if they once again squander their\x0d\nresources, salvation may only be\x0d\ntemporary.\x0d\n\x0d\nBut fate will decide whether history repeats\x0d\nitself...
large	And so the intrepid explorers succeed in\x0d\nsecuring a healthy supply of edible matter\x0d\nfor their home planet.\x0d\n\x0d\nIf they carefully cultivate the seeds they've\x0d\nharvested, it will surely bring an end to\x0d\nKoppai's food-supply crisis.\x0d\n\x0d\nAnd, while brief, the explorers' time\x0d\nworking together with the Pikmin has\x0d\ntaught them the wisdom of "planning."\x0d\n\x0d\nThat wisdom will be the key to harnessing\x0d\nthese newfound resources.\x0d\n\x0d\nSimply put, their fate is in their own hands.
perfect	And so the intrepid explorers successfully\x0d\ncomplete their mission!\x0d\n\x0d\nAfter securing a bountiful supply of edible\x0d\nmatter and learning the valuable lessons of\x0d\n"planning" and "teamwork," the explorers\x0d\nare set to become the saviors of their\x0d\nhome planet.\x0d\n\x0d\nUnder their guidance, the seeds they've\x0d\nrecovered will be used to kick off a\x0d\nsustainable cycle of cultivation and\x0d\nharvesting, thus bringing new life to\x0d\nKoppai.\x0d\n\x0d\nHowever, one question remains.
